This gift is said tohave been made by the donor in gratitude for thebirth of a son to him called Kempē-Vīra-Gauḍa.

NANGUNERI TALUK
2
Placement
Dalapatisamudram.--On thenorth and west walls of thecentral shrine in the Tirunāgēś-vara temple at the village.
Year
Pāṇḍya
King
Māṟavarman alias TribhuvanchakravartinSundara-Pāṇḍyadēva, ‘who was pleasedto present the Chōḷa country’.
Date
8th year and 239thday.
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
Begins with the introduction pUmaruviya tirumaTantaietc. Records that at the request of the Śivabrāhmaṇas andSthānapatis of the temple of Tirunāgēśvaram at Perumba-ḻañji in Nāṭṭāṟṟuppōkku and of the queen Ulaga-muḻuduḍaiyāḷ, the king, while seated on the thronecalled Maḻavarāyaṉ at Madura, exempted from taxescertain lands, to provide for offerings and worship to theimages of Kūttāḍundēvar and his consort, set up in thetemple by Kaṇṇaṉ-Kōvaṉ alias Vīranārāyaṇadēvaṉ.

Registers a grant of land made at the request of Mahāpra-dhāna Saṁkharayya-Nāyaka and the Maneverggaḍe Madhu-vapayya-Nāyaka, by Trailōkyamalla Vīra-Noḷamba-pallava-Permāḍi Jayasiṁghadēva to the big tank atMoraba, which was named Noḷamba-samudra, when hewas governing Kandūr--1,000, Puligeṟe--300 andBeḷvola-300 as Yuvarāja. It is stated that the grantwas made on the occasion of his performing the rites ofHiraṇyagarbha and Tulāpurusha, while he was encampedat the nelevīḍu of E1tagiri.

Date
Śaka 981, Vikāri,Mārgaśira, śu. 2,Wednesday,Pūrvāshāḍha,Kaulava-karaṇa,Gaṇḍa-Tōga.
Language and Script
Sanskṛit & Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records the death, by saṁnyasana-vidhi in the Ghaṭānta-kiya-basadi at Moraṁba, of the Jaina teacher Nāga-chandra-Siddhāntadēva, a disciple of Jayakīrttidēva ofthe Yāpanīya-saṁgha. Nāgachandra-yati is praised as agreat scholar and is given the biruda of Mantrachūḍā-maṇi. The nisidhi stone (on which the inscription isincised) was set up by his disciple Kanakaśakti-Siddhān-tadēva.
